## nature-lang/nature

> `#Custom Compiler` `#Coroutines` `#Garbage Collection` `#Systems Programming` `#c` `#compiler` `#hacktoberfest` `#lang` `#language` `#nature` `#programming-language` 
> Nature is a general-purpose systems programming language with a pure C self-developed compiler generating native machine code without LLVM dependency. It features built-in concurrency primitives, high-performance GC with minimal STW, shared-stack coroutines capable of millions of switches per second, and tcmalloc-style memory allocation. Supports cross-platform deployment via static musl libc linking with comprehensive type system including generics, tagged unions, interfaces, and zero-overhead C FFI.
> <sub>The Nature Programming Language</sub>

> Cosmopolitan Libc transforms C/C++ into a build-once run-anywhere language that runs natively on Linux, Mac, Windows, FreeBSD, OpenBSD, NetBSD, and BIOS without requiring an interpreter or VM. By reconfiguring GCC/Clang to output APE (Actually Portable Executable) format, it achieves cross-platform compatibility with minimal footprint (as small as 12KB), featuring built-in strace and ftrace debugging capabilities.
> <sub>build-once run-anywhere c library</sub>

## tporadowski/redis

> [!info]
> ⭐ 10,011 · C · 2023-04-02  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/tporadowski/redis) · [Website](http://redis.io)  
> `#Windows Port` `#In-Memory Database` `#Redis Fork` `# Jemalloc` `#redis` `#redis-for-windows` `#redis-msi-installer` `#redis-windows` `#redis-windows-installer` `#redis-windows-native` `#redis-windows-service` 
> This is an unofficial native port of Redis for Windows x64, bringing the high-performance in-memory database to Windows platforms. The project provides Redis 4.0.14 and 5.0.14 with full support for all data types including Strings, Lists, Sets, Sorted Sets, Hashes, and Streams. It uses a customized jemalloc allocator to handle Windows memory management for RDB/AOF persistence, requiring Visual Studio 2019 for building.
> <sub>Native port of Redis for Windows. Redis is an in-memory database that persists on disk. The data model is key-value, but many different kind of values are supported: Strings, Lists, Sets, Sorted Sets, Hashes, Streams, HyperLogLogs. This repository contains unofficial port of Redis to Windows.</sub>

> `#Diffusion Models` `#Multilingual Text Generation` `#Visual Text Editing` `#OCR Glyph Encoding` 
> AnyText is a diffusion-based framework for multilingual visual text generation and editing. It combines an auxiliary latent module with a text embedding module, leveraging OCR stroke encoding and image caption embeddings to seamlessly integrate generated text into backgrounds. Using text-control diffusion loss and text perceptual loss, it achieves high writing accuracy. Supports text generation, editing, and community model weight merging. Accepted by ICLR 2024 Spotlight.
> <sub>Official implementation code of the paper <AnyText: Multilingual Visual Text Generation And Editing></sub>

## lllyasviel/ControlNet

> [!info]
> ⭐ 33,687 · Python · 2024-02-25  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/lllyasviel/ControlNet)  
> `#Diffusion Model Control` `#Zero Convolution` `#Conditional Image Generation` `#Stable Diffusion` 
> ControlNet is a neural network structure that controls text-to-image diffusion models by adding extra conditions. It duplicates network weights into locked and trainable copies, using zero-convolution to avoid interfering with the original model during initial training. This enables fine-tuning with small image pair datasets while reusing Stable Diffusion as a powerful backbone. The project supports edge detection, depth estimation, pose estimation, and provides low VRAM mode for consumer GPUs.
> <sub>Let us control diffusion models!</sub>

## apache/incubator-seata

> [!info]

> `#Distributed Transaction` `#Microservices` `#AT Mode` `#Transaction Coordinator` `#at` `#consistency` `#distributed-transaction` `#microservice` `#saga` `#tcc` `#xa` 
> Seata is an Apache incubating distributed transaction solution designed for microservices architecture. It supports four transaction modes: AT, TCC, Saga, and XA, coordinating global and branch transactions through a three-role model (TC, TM, RM) to ensure data consistency across services. With high performance, easy integration, and low intrusion, it is widely used in finance, e-commerce, logistics and other data-critical scenarios.

> Uperf is an Android userspace performance controller managing CPU frequency and scheduling via sysfs nodes. Its core features include dynamic performance adjustment based on app scenarios, UI thread binding to big cores, touch screen input monitoring for tap boost, and active system load sampling to detect heavy workloads. Compatible with Android 6.0-12 and arm64 architecture, supports Magisk or manual installation without dependency on system frameworks or specific kernels.
> <sub>Userspace performance controller for android</sub>
